(the &#8220;Company&#8221;) that he will resign from the Board effective immediately.</span></div><div style="text-align:justify"><span><br/></span></div><div style="text-align:justify"><span style="color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:10pt;font-weight:400;line-height:120%">Mr. Call served on the Board as a designee of Mondel&#275;z International, Inc. (&#8220;Mondel&#275;z&#8221;), a stockholder of the Company, pursuant to the terms of the Investor Rights Agreement, dated as of July 9, 2018, by and among the Company, Maple Holdings B.V. and Mondel&#275;z (the &#8220;Investor Rights Agreement&#8221;). The Investor Rights Agreement entitles Mondel&#275;z to designate a director to the Company&#8217;s Board, provided it beneficially owns at least 5% of the Company&#8217;s common stock. Given that Mondel&#275;z&#8217;s ownership has fallen below 5%, Mr. Call has resigned, and Mondel&#275;z is no longer entitled to designate any directors to the Company&#8217;s Board. Mr. Call&#8217;s decision to resign did not result from any disagreement with the Company or the Board.
